<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="A6L_e-tron">A6L e-tron</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Audi_A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: A6L e-tron">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_02_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="689" data-file-width="1300" height="117" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_02_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg/220px-Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_02_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_02_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg/330px-Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_02_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_02_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg/440px-Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_02_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_02_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Audi A6L e-tron at <a href="/wiki/Auto_Shanghai" title="Auto Shanghai">Auto Shanghai</a> 2015</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_05_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="690" data-file-width="1300" height="117" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_05_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg/220px-Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_05_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_05_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg/330px-Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_05_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_05_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg/440px-Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_05_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Audi_A6L_C7_e-tron_05_--_Auto_Shanghai_--_2015-04-22.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Audi A6L e-tron at <a href="/wiki/Auto_Shanghai" title="Auto Shanghai">Auto Shanghai</a> 2015</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The concept vehicle was unveiled in <a href="/wiki/Auto_China" title="Auto China">Auto China</a> 2012 in Beijing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup></p>
<p>It is a <a href="/wiki/Plug-in_hybrid" title="Plug-in hybrid">plug-in hybrid</a> version of A6 L with <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=2.0_TFSI&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="2.0 TFSI (page does not exist)">2.0 TFSI</a> 211 PS (155 kW) engine combined with a 95 PS (70 kW) electric motor. Electric power is supplied via <a href="/wiki/Lithium-ion_battery" title="Lithium-ion battery">lithium-ion battery</a>, with <a href="/wiki/All-electric_range" title="All-electric range">all-electric range</a> of 80 km (49.71 mi) for constant 60 km/h (37.28 mph) drive. Other features include MMI navigation plus developed in Audi Infotainment Tech Center (ITC) in Beijing.</p>
<p>The series production plug-in hybrid car will be available in China in 2016 on the long-wheelbase version, using the same <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hybrid_vehicle_powertrain" title="Hybrid vehicle powertrain">hybrid vehicle powertrain</a> like the concept vehicle. Output of 180 kW (245 hp), with 500 Nm maximum torque, all-electric range will be 50 km (31.1 mi). Acceleration from 0–60 mph in 8,4 seconds. Fuel consumption will be 2,2 l/100 km (106.9 US mpg).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="A6_Black_Edition_.282013.E2.80.93.29">A6 Black Edition (2013–)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Audi_A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: A6 Black Edition (2013–)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Available in Saloon and Avant bodies, they are versions of A6 S line with 177PS 2.0-litre TDI or higher engines (excluding S6) in front-wheel-drive or quattro all-wheel-drive configurations, for the UK market. It included 20-inch rotor-design alloy wheels with a dark titanium finish, black grille and number plate surrounds and the window frame strips, and by privacy glass extending from the B-pillar rearwards; black roof rails Piano Black inlays, sports seats upholstered in black Valcona leather, black headlining, BOSE audio system with DAB radio, Audi Music Interface (AMI) for iPod connection.</p>
<p>Sales began in November 2012, with deliveries began in early 2013.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="RS_6_Avant_.282013.E2.80.93.29">RS 6 Avant (2013–)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Audi_A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: RS 6 Avant (2013–)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot_(1).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot_%281%29.jpg/220px-Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot_%281%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot_%281%29.jpg/330px-Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot_%281%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot_%281%29.jpg/440px-Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot_%281%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot_(1).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
RS 6 Avant</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot.jpg/220px-Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot.jpg/330px-Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot.jpg/440px-Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Audi_RS6_-_Flickr_-_Alexandre_Pr%C3%A9vot.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
RS 6 Avant</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>It is a version of S6 Avant with increased engine power to 560 PS (412 kW; 552 hp)@5700–6700rpm and 700 N·m (516.29 lbf·ft)@1750–5500rpm, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cylinder_on_demand" title="Cylinder on demand">cylinder on demand</a> system deactivates intake and exhaust valves of 4 cylinders (2, 3, 5 and 8), eight-speed tiptronic transmission with shortened shift times and D and S driving modes, quattro permanent all-wheel drive system with torque vectoring with self-locking center differential with an elevated locking value and oil cooler, adaptive air suspension lowering body by 20 mm (1 in) (optional tauter sport suspension plus with <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dynamic_Ride_Control&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dynamic Ride Control (page does not exist)">Dynamic Ride Control</a>), option is dynamic steering, four internally vented 390 mm (15 in) diameter brake discs in wave design with a wave-like outer contour (optional 420 mm (17 in) diameter carbon fiber-ceramic brake discs with anthracite gray calipers), black six-piston brake calipers (optional red brake calipers), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Electronic_stabilization_control" title="Electronic stabilization control">electronic stabilization control</a> with Sport and off modes, high-gloss 20-inch forged wheels in a seven twin-spoke design (optional 21-inch cast wheels in high-gloss silver, polished black or polished titanium-look), matte aluminum applications on the body, high-gloss black protective grille at the front of the car, the bumpers, the fender, sill flares and the large roof spoiler; rear diffuser with two large elliptical exhaust tailpipes, a choice of 9 body colours (including exclusive shade Daytona Gray matte), dial instruments feature black faces and white dials and red needles, flat-bottomed three-spoke multifunction steering wheel, illuminated entry sills, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Driver_information_system&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Driver information system (page does not exist)">driver information system</a> (DIS) sport RS logos, RS 6-specific driver information system, footrest and pedals and switches in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MMI_navigation_plus" title="MMI navigation plus">MMI navigation plus</a> terminal in aluminum finish, decorative bezel surrounding the retractable monitor in a piano finish, interior door openers in a delicate double-bar design, standard Carbon inlays (with six additional materials as options), standard black headlining (optional Silver or black Alcantara), RS sport seats with side bolsters and integrated head restraints and RS 6 logos upholstered in black Alcantara and leather with diamond quilting at center sections (optional honeycomb-quilted Valcona leather in either black or Moon Silver), optional power-adjustable deluxe seats with memory function, two sportily molded rear seats (optional three-person bench seat), xenon plus headlights, LED rear lights, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tire-pressure_control_system" title="Tire-pressure control system">tire-pressure control system</a>, illuminated entry sills, custom driver-information system, parking system plus, cruise control, three-zone automatic air conditioning, MMI navigation plus with MMI touch and the 10-speaker Audi sound system.</p>
<p>Optional appearance packages (in Matte Aluminum or Carbon) includes customized quattro badges on the central front air inlet. Carbon appearance package includes alternate front splitter and diffuser shapes. Optional Dynamic package increases top speed to 280 km/h (173.98 mph). Optional Dynamic plus package increases top speed to 305 km/h (189.52 mph). Other options include <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LED_headlight" title="LED headlight">LED headlights</a> with a unique design, the sport differential on the rear axle, Comfort package, <a href="/wiki/Head-up_display" title="Head-up display">head-up display</a>, the high-performance driver assistance systems, Bang &amp; Olufsen Advanced Sound System with 15 speakers and 1,200 watts of total power, Bluetooth online <a href="/wiki/Car_phone" title="Car phone">car phone</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup></p>
<p>UK model was available to order from early 2013, with deliveries beginning in next summer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup></p>

<p>A6L with 2.0 TFSI (180PS) was sold as A6L TFSI in China.</p>
<p>In USA, Canada, UK A6 Saloon with 3.0 TFSI quattro (310PS) replaced the A6 3.0 TFSI quattro (300PS).</p>
<p>In UK, A6 Avant with 3.0 TFSI quattro (310PS) replaced the A6 3.0 TFSI quattro (300PS).</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Safety_2">Safety</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Audi_A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Safety">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div>
<table class="wikitable">
<tr>
<th colspan="3"><a href="/wiki/Euro_NCAP" title="Euro NCAP">Euro NCAP</a> test results</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="3" style="text-align:center;">LHD, 4-door saloon (2011)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EuroNCAP2011_59-0"><a href="#cite_note-EuroNCAP2011-59">[59]</a></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th>Test</th>
<th>Points</th>
<th>%</th>
</tr>

<td>Overall:</td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marketing">Marketing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Audi_A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Marketing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As part of Audi A6 Avant launch in the UK, BBH London, Knucklehead, The Whitehouse, The Mill produced the 'Hummingbird' TV commercial, directed by Daniel Barber. The commercial premiered on Saturday 2011-10-01 during ITV1's coverage of the Rugby World Cup. The commercial was to imagine what a bird designed by Audi would look like and to reflect the car's ultra-lightweight technology. Johann Strauss's 'Open Road, Open Sky' was sung by legendary American baritone and automobile lover John Charles Thomas. In addition, 60 second and 30 versions of the ads were supported by press, print and radio campaigns, as well as a presence on the Daily Telegraph's iPad app.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup></p>
<p>As part of Audi A6 launch in Taiwan, 2011 Audi Fashion Festival featured the theme of 'A6- The sum of Progress', including Shiatzy Chen, Kiki Huang, Robyn Hung and an artistic jewelry brand, Chen Chan.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup></p>
<p>As part of 2013 Audi S6 sedan launch in the US market, 3 different versions of 'Prom' commercial were premiered during 2013 Super Bowl game.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup> The 60-second ad, created by Venables Bell &amp; Partners, features a teenage boy. Voters were to decide their favourite version of the commercial 24 hours on Friday before the Super Bowl game, with winning entry shown on Saturday at Audi's YouTube channel and during the actual game at CBS.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup></p>
<p>As part of RS 6 Avant launch, Audi Land of quattro Alpen Tour 2013 featured RS 6 Avant begins on September 23, travelling across twelve driving stages in 6 countries (Klagenfurt – the capital of Carinthia, Austria, Monaco).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup></p>
<p>In the Audi RS 6 Avant TV commercial titled 'Perfect Fit', it featured a 2012 Audi R18 with the high downforce sprint bodywork in the guise of Audi R18 e-tron quattro.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Use_in_China">Use in China</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Audi_A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Use in China">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>According to <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dunne_%26_Company&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dunne &amp; Company (page does not exist)">Dunne &amp; Company</a>, a research company, as of 2011, purchases in China and Hong Kong make up about half of the 229,200 Audi A6s sold in the world. By 2012 many government officials in China began driving with Audi A6s. After a 1994 campaign from the Chinese government to have officials stop driving Mercedes stretch limousines, the officials began using black Audi A6 cars. Michael Wines of <i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i> wrote that "More than a perk, the black Audi is a rolling advertisement for its occupant’s importance and impunity in a nation obsessed with status."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup></p>
